Category Definitions (based on a 36-epoch analysis window):
- Healthy: A pool with >= 3M ADA in stake AND its pledge is met.
- Viable but Small: A pool with < 3M ADA, has earned >= 5500 ADA in rewards, AND its pledge is met.
- Struggling: An active pool that does not meet the criteria for Healthy, Viable but Small, or Inactive.
- Inactive: A pool is classified as Inactive if it is not viable and meets EITHER of these conditions:
    a) It has an Unmet Pledge AND at least one other signal of neglect (No Update or No Governance).
    b) It has 0 blocks, is a statistical underperformer (or has negligible stake), AND triggers at least one other signal of neglect.

Signal Key:
- UP: Unmet Pledge
- ZB: Zero Blocks in 6 Months
- NU: No Update in >1 Year
- NG: No Governance Participation
